35const int ifac[N] = {1,1,499122177,166374059,291154603,856826403,641926577,376916469,421456191,712324701,370705776,305948985};
36
37inline int C(int n, int k) {
38 int ans = 1;
39 FOR(i,0,k-1) ans = 1ll * ans * (n-i) % p;
40 return 1ll * ans * ifac[k] % p;
41}
42
43inline void sol() {
44 int n, k, x;
45 cin >> n >> k >> x;
46 int ans = 0;
47 FOR(l,1,min(n,M-1)) FOR(c,1,N-1) {
48 int cur = f[k][x][l][c];
49 if (!cur) continue;
50 err("%d %d = %d ", l, c, cur);
51 cur = 1ll * cur * C(n-l+c,c) % p;
52 err("%d\n", cur);
53 ans = (ans + cur) % p;
54 }
55 O(ans);
56}
57
58int main() {
59#ifndef MISAKA
60#ifdef IOFILE
61 freopen(IOFILE ".in", "r", stdin);
62 freopen(IOFILE ".out", "w", stdout);
63#endif
64 ios::sync_with_stdio(0);
65 cin.tie(0);
66#endif
67#ifdef MULTI
68 int T;
69 cin >> T;
70 while (T--)
71#endif
72 sol();
73 return 0;
74}
